\DoxyCodeLine{2211   \textcolor{comment}{// We potentially use lookahead in order to determine the return type in case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2212   \textcolor{comment}{// it is not yet clear from the call context. Special care has to be taken to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2213   \textcolor{comment}{// ensure the non-\/contextual lookahead is valid. The following restrictions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2214   \textcolor{comment}{// substantiate the validity of the lookahead implemented below:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2215   \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ All calls (except stdlib calls) require some sort of type annotation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2216   \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ The coercion to "{}signed"{} is part of the \{BitwiseORExpression\}, any}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2217   \textcolor{comment}{//    intermittent expressions like parenthesis in `(callsite(..))|0` are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2218   \textcolor{comment}{//    syntactically not considered coercions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2219   \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ The coercion to "{}double"{} as part of the \{UnaryExpression\} has higher}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2220   \textcolor{comment}{//    precedence and wins in `+callsite(..)|0` cases. Only "{}float"{} return}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2221   \textcolor{comment}{//    types are overridden in `fround(callsite(..)|0)` expressions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2222   \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Expected coercions to "{}signed"{} are flagged via \{call\_coercion\_deferred\}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2223   \textcolor{comment}{//    and later on validated as part of \{BitwiseORExpression\} to ensure they}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2224   \textcolor{comment}{//    indeed apply to the current call expression.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2225   \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ The deferred validation is only allowed if \{BitwiseORExpression\} did}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2226   \textcolor{comment}{//    promise to fulfill the request via \{call\_coercion\_deferred\_position\}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2227   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (allow\_peek \&\& \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1internal_1_1wasm_1_1AsmJsParser_a167dcbd959dcac1611060b875c9aa358}{Peek}}(\textcolor{charliteral}{'|'}) \&\&}
\DoxyCodeLine{2228       function\_info-\/>kind <= \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1internal_1_1wasm_1_1AsmJsParser_aa3f92d02c72dbeaec2ef9dfdf6def252aa700cada361d9f5601074180fb1ee256}{VarKind::kImportedFunction}} \&\&}
